They also play a crucial role in flood control, absorbing excess water during heavy rainfall. The wetlands in Helen are teeming with unique plant species, including cattails, reeds, and water lilies, which contribute to the area's natural beauty.<br/><br/>Surrounding the water bodies and wetlands, Helen boasts lush green forests and woodlands. These forests are predominantly composed of hardwood trees such as oak, maple, and hickory. The forests are home to a variety of wildlife, including deer, foxes, and a wide array of bird species.<br/><br/>The town's geography is also influenced by its proximity to the Chesapeake Bay, which lies to the east. Tacaíonn an éiceachóras éagsúil uisceach le réimse leathan flóra agus fána, rud a fhágann gur áit iontach é Helen do dhíograiseoirí dúlra agus do lucht féachana éin.<br/><br/>Taobh amuigh de na comhlachtaí uisce, tá Helen beannaithe le bogaigh fhairsing freisin.Tá na bogaigh seo ina éiceachóras ríthábhachtach a thacaíonn le héagsúlacht plandaí agus ainmhithe. Feidhmíonn bogaigh mar scagairí nádúrtha, ag íonú uisce agus ag feabhsú a cháilíocht. Tá ról ríthábhachtach acu freisin maidir le rialú tuile, ionsúnn siad an t-uisce breise le linn báisteach throm.Tá na bogaigh i Helen ag cur faoi deara le speicis plandaí uathúla, lena n-áirítear caititiúla, giolcacha, agus lilí uisce, a chuireann le háilleacht nádúrtha an cheantair.<br/><br/>Tá foraoisí glasa agus coillearnacha lush ag Helen agus a bhfuil na foraoisí seo comhdhéanta den chuid is mó de chrainn crua ar nós dair, mapaí agus heicor. Soláthraíonn an clúdach foraoise dlúth scáth agus atmaisféar fionnuar, ag tabhairt cuireadh do chónaitheoirí agus do chuairteoirí iniúchadh a dhéanamh ar an timpeallacht nádúrtha.Tá éagsúlacht fiadhúlra, fianna, sionnaigh san áireamh, agus raon leathan speiceas éan sna foraoisí.<br/><br/>Bíonn tionchar ag an ngeografaíocht baile freisin ar a ngaireacht don Chaespake Bay, atá suite san oirthear.Is é an Cuan Seapak an t-inbhear is mó sna Stáit Aontaithe agus is eol dó mar gheall ar a bhithéagsúlacht agus a thábhacht éiceolaíoch. Tugann a chóngar do Helen deis do chónaitheoirí agus do chuairteoirí rochtain a fháil ar an bhá, ag cur deiseanna ar fáil dóibh chun dul ar bhád, chun iascaireacht agus iniúchadh a dhéanamh ar go leor oileán agus tránna an bhá.<br/><br/>Ar an iomlán, cuireann tíreolaíocht Helen, Maryland meascán comhchuí de chomhlachtaí uisce, bogaigh agus foraoisí ar fáil. Fágann áilleacht nádúrtha agus éiceachórais éagsúla an bhaile gur ceann scríbe tarraingteach é do dhíograiseoirí lasmuigh, do dhaoine a bhfuil grá acu don dúlra, agus dóibh siúd atá ag lorg cúlráid shíochánta. Cibé an bhfuil sé ag iniúchadh an Cnaipí Abhainn, ag breathnú ar fhiadhúlra sna bogaigh, nó ag siúl trí fhoraoisí radhairc, cuireann Helen eispéireas uathúil tarraingteach ar fáil do gach duine a théann isteach ina thíreolaíocht.<br/><br/>Stair, Eacnamaíocht agus Polaitíocht Helen, Maryland<br/><br/>Baile beag atá i nDomhnachnach le chéile in oirthuaisceart na Stát Aontaithe.Cé go mb’fhéidir nach bhfuil stair shaibhir, geilleagar éagsúil, agus tírdhreach polaitiúil spéisiúil ann a mhúnlaigh a fhorbairt thar na blianta.<br/><br/>Téann stair Helen siar go dtí tús an 17ú haois nuair a tháinig na lonnaitheoirí Eorpacha go dtí an ceantar ar dtús. Bhí cónaí ar an mbaile i dtosach ag treibheanna Meiriceánach Dúchasacha, lena n-áirítear muintir na Nanticoke agus Piscataway. D'eascair athruithe suntasacha ar an réigiún as an gcoilíneacht Eorpach, agus bunú feirmeacha, muilte agus poist trádála.<br/><br/>Ag deireadh an 18ú haois, thosaigh Helen ag bláthú mar mhol talmhaíochta, agus d’fhás feirmeoirí barra mar thobac, arbhar agus cruithneacht. De bharr suíomh straitéiseach an bhaile ar bhruach an Oirthir, bhí sé ina phríomh-mhol iompair, agus bhí earraí á n-iompar tríd an gCótan Abhann agus ar iarnród níos déanaí. Mar thoradh air sin tháinig fás an gheilleagair áitiúil ar an ngeilleagar áitiúil agus ar bhunú gnólachtaí beaga agus tionscail.<br/><br/>Tá geilleagar Helen éagsúil le himeacht ama. Cé gur earnáil thábhachtach í an talmhaíocht, tá fás le feiceáil i dtionscail amhail déantúsaíocht, turasóireacht agus seirbhísí. Déanann an talamh torthúil agus an aeráid fabhrach Helen a chabhródh leis an fheirmeoireacht, le fócas ar bharra cosúil le arbhar, pónairí soighe, agus glasraí. Ina theannta sin, tá dlúthbhaint ag an mbaile le cathracha móra mar Baltimore agus Washington, D.C., ag oscailt deiseanna do ghnólachtaí beaga atá ag freastal ar thurasóirí agus ar chomaitéirí.<br/><br/>Le blianta beaga anuas, tá tionscal na turasóireachta tar éis ardcháil air i Helen. Tá tírdhreach pictiúrtha an bhaile, foirgnimh stairiúla a fheictear, agus cuairteoirí a mhealladh chuig áiteanna i gcéin. Tá infheistíocht déanta ag an rialtas áitiúil i gcur chun cinn na turasóireachta, féilte a eagrú, agus suíomhanna stairiúla a chaomhnú chun borradh a chur faoin ngeilleagar áitiúil.<br/><br/>Ar bhonn polaitiúil, is cuid de Chontae Chúil Mhín í Helen agus tagann sí faoi rialú oifigigh tofa. Feidhmíonn an baile faoi fhoirm rialtais méara-Chomhairle, agus é mar phríomhfheidhmeannach agus mar phríomh-chomhairleoir atá freagrach as cinntí beartais a dhéanamh. Tá ról ríthábhachtach ag toghcháin áitiúla maidir le ceannaireacht pholaitiúil an bhaile a chinneadh agus a bheartais a mhúnlú.<br/><br/>Cosúil le go leor bailte beaga, bhí air na coraí eacnamaíocha, athruithe i ndéimeagrafaic a nascleanúint, agus saincheisteanna sóisialta atá ag athrú a nascleanúint. Tá an rialtas áitiúil ag díriú ar fhorbairt inbhuanaithe a chur chun cinn, tacú le gnólachtaí áitiúla, agus ar bhonneagar a fheabhsú chun aghaidh a thabhairt ar na dúshláin sin.<br/><br/>Le blianta beaga anuas, tá béim níos mó anois ar chaomhnú agus ar inbhuanaitheacht chomhshaoil le feiceáil ag Helen agus rinneadh iarrachtaí chun acmhainní nádúrtha an réigiúin a chosaint, Cuan Cheskea agus a chuid fo-aibhneacha san áireamh. Tá bearta curtha i bhfeidhm ag an mbaile chun truailliú a laghdú, fuinneamh in-athnuaite a chur chun cinn, agus éiceathurasóireacht a spreagadh.<br/><br/>Mar fhocal scoir, féadfaidh Helen, Maryland, a bheith ina bhaile beag, ach tá stair shaibhir aige, geilleagar éagsúil, agus tírdhreach polaitiúil atá ag athrú. Ón lá tosaigh i leith an tionscail ar mhaithe le cúrsaí turasóireachta agus inbhuanaitheacht, tá Helen in oiriúint d’amanna a athrú fad is a chaomhnaíonn a charm uathúil. Agus an baile ag fás i gcónaí agus ag mealladh cuairteoirí, beidh sé suimiúil a fheiceáil conas a fhorbraíonn a gheilleagar agus a thírdhreach polaitiúil amach anseo. |

| This website stores data such as cookies to enable essential site functionality, as well as marketing, personalization, and analytics. By remaining on this website, you indicate your consent. Cookie Policy<br/><br/>'Look at me now': Using neuroscience to help at-risk kids — and change Maryland's juvenile justice system<br/><br/>Thank you for supporting our journalism. This article is available exclusively for our subscribers, who help fund our work at The Baltimore Sun.<br/><br/>Image 1 of 9<br/><br/>Paul Finley, employment specialist with Roca Baltimore, speaks to young men in the program. Roca staff works with young men involved with the justice system using CBT, cognitive behavioral therapy, to help them change their thinking patterns and behaviors. (Kim Hairston/Baltimore Sun )<br/><br/>Raynold Smith was beefing with another man for months and when they crossed paths in March 2021, both were armed.<br/><br/>The reason Smith didn't pull the trigger? In a split-second moment, when life and death hung in the balance, he glimpsed a child's car seat and suddenly realized everything his enemy stood to lose. Almost immediately, Smith felt a bullet rip through his leg, narrowly missing a major artery and immobilizing him for weeks.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>That was the second time Smith, 26, of Baltimore, had been shot; a 2019 shooting left him with graze wounds. He knew something had to change.<br/><br/>Over the next several months, he found what he needed at Roca, a nonprofit anti-violence program in Baltimore. In addition to job training and life skills classes, the program helps teens and young men recover from trauma and forge a new path — by rewiring their brains.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>For that, Roca uses what it calls cognitive behavioral therapy, which focuses on examining the relationship of thoughts, emotions and actions. The theory is relatively simple, but the results can be profound, according to program staff and participants.<br/><br/>Could expanding the use of CBT among vulnerable youth help decrease gun violence and create healthier, more resilient communities? Experts and officials are optimistic, and the Maryland Department of Juvenile Services, in partnership with Roca, plans to find out.<br/><br/>Calvin Monroe, left, a Roca Baltimore youth worker, hugs Raynold Smith, 26, after checking in with him. Roca staff members work with young men involved with the justice system using cognitive behavioral therapy. Roca will be training Maryland Department of Juvenile Services staff in CBT to use with kids in the juvenile justice system. (Kim Hairston/Baltimore Sun )<br/><br/>Earlier this year, department leaders announced that 300 staff members — including many who work with the roughly 1,000 young people on either juvenile probation or post-release supervision — would receive training from Roca on adolescent brain science, the psychology of trauma and CBT.<br/><br/>A nearly $1 million federal grant will pay for the training, which comes amid a widespread push for juvenile justice reform. The General Assembly passed a series of bills this year with that goal, including eliminating youth confinement for most first-time misdemeanors, setting minimum age requirements for criminal charges and limiting the length of juvenile probation terms.<br/><br/>"Baltimore has a lot of hurt and pain," said Ronnetta Alexander, a juvenile services case manager supervisor who recently completed the training. "This better prepares us to go in and assist these families. It opens the door to show them there really is a different choice."<br/><br/>Smith's split-second decision foreshadowed the skills he's since solidified. He thought about the potential consequences — a child caught in the crossfire — and didn't shoot. Now, he understands it in the context of one of CBT's tenets: "Act on your values."<br/><br/>He recently applied it in another volatile situation. He suspected infidelity in a relationship, got angry and was inclined toward violence. Then he considered all he stood to lose: his freedom, his kids, his two jobs. With the language to articulate his decision and a support system, stepping away was easier this time: "Some stuff is really not worth it," he said, shrugging.<br/><br/>Instead, he picked up more shifts, often working seven days a week between the shipping department of a graphics company in Timonium and as a food runner at the Baltimore Comedy Factory.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>Raynold Smith, at left, and Calvin Monroe, a Roca Baltimore youth worker, speak about issues Smith is dealing with. Roca staff members work with young men involved with the justice system using cognitive behavioral therapy, or CBT, to help them change their thinking patterns and behaviors. (Kim Hairston/Baltimore Sun )<br/><br/>Smith said he believes either a police officer or social worker referred him to Roca after meeting with him in the hospital after he got shot last year.<br/><br/>Through CBT and his close relationship with Calvin Monroe, the Roca worker assigned to his case, Smith credited the program with keeping him calm and levelheaded. The stress of past trauma still puts him on edge, but Smith said labeling his emotions allows him to avoid impulsive actions he might regret.<br/><br/>Standing outside his apartment complex during a recent check-in with Monroe, Smith joked about becoming a homebody: doing chores and staying safe.<br/><br/>Monroe said a huge challenge is getting young men to leave the streets — where the promise of fast money often outweighs the threat of violence — and choose long-term stability, even if that means making minimum wage or having to take high school equivalency classes.<br/><br/>"There's no retirement plan in the streets. It's either death or jail," Monroe said. "That's what I keep telling them."<br/><br/>Changes in the brain<br/><br/>The program that Roca developed focuses on identifying "Think-Feel-Do" cycles and disrupting them to avoid potential negative outcomes. From a neuroscience perspective, that often means forging new pathways in the brain and strengthening them over time.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>Founded in Massachusetts more than 30 years ago, Roca opened its Baltimore office in 2018. It has a reputation for success with some of the city's most troubled and potentially dangerous young men.<br/><br/>The program teaches seven skills to disrupt unhealthy cycles. The first is to "Be present," instead of fixating on the past or future, staff members said. Others include "Label your feelings," "Stick with it" and "Flex your thinking."<br/><br/>Experts say this type of therapy can be beneficial for people recovering from trauma, because they spend more time in "fight or flight" mode.<br/><br/>When people experience frequent trauma — such as regularly seeing gun violence — their brain activity changes to reflect a heightened sense of danger. That creates more activity in the amygdala, the region associated with fear and stress responses, and less in the prefrontal cortex. That's where reasoning helps regulate emotions and impulses, leading to slower, more careful decision-making. For most people, the prefrontal cortex takes the longest to develop, reaching maturity around age 25.<br/><br/>During a summit last month hosted by the University of Maryland School of Medicine in Baltimore, Democratic Mayor Brandon Scott said he was 7 the first time he saw someone get shot.<br/><br/>"Growing up young and Black in Park Heights, living with the trauma of gun violence — everyone I knew had the same experiences. We thought that was normal," he said. "We have to really think about how that impacts someone's brain."<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>Dr. Kerry Ressler, a professor of psychiatry at Harvard Medical School, said rates of post-traumatic stress disorder are higher in some urban neighborhoods than among military veterans.<br/><br/>"From a psychiatric perspective, people really are living in war zones," he said at the summit. "People are getting in trouble and contributing to cycles of violence in part because of untreated trauma."<br/><br/>Treatments like CBT can result in measurable changes to brain activity that promote healthier outcomes, he said.<br/><br/>'This gives them emotional equity'<br/><br/>In the Maryland Department of Juvenile Services, staff in Baltimore were the first to undergo Roca's ReWire CBT training; eventually, it will extend statewide.<br/><br/>Some were skeptical at first, doubtful that an 11-week training program on psychological theory would translate to improved interactions with the children they supervise. But at some point, the light bulb went off for Justine Buckingham, a juvenile services case manager supervisor.<br/><br/>Now, she often pulls out a worksheet to help her clients explore interconnected thoughts, feelings and actions. For example, she pointed to a diagram by a young man who was having problems at school. Thinking he didn't know enough to pass a test made him feel nervous and disappointed, which led him to skip school and get in trouble.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>Identifying that cycle allowed him to envision another outcome, Buckingham said. What if he studied enough to pass his classes? Then he could be proud, stay in school and earn his diploma. The skill he chose to focus on: "Stick with it."<br/><br/>Young people hold themselves accountable this way, she said, rather than just complying with a judge's orders.<br/><br/>"These kids have been told so much about who they are, what they will become or not become. But they've never been given a road map," said James "JT" Timpson, director of community partnerships at Roca Maryland. "This gives them emotional equity. It gives them control without taking away accountability."<br/><br/>Jenny Egan, who oversees the Baltimore juvenile division for the Maryland Office of the Public Defender, said the initiative is overdue, though she disputed whether it should be labeled cognitive behavioral therapy, a clinical term referring to a type of psychological treatment. Nonetheless, she said the evidence-based approach is a first step toward improving outcomes for vulnerable youth.<br/><br/>"This system is supposed to be about offering kids support, guidance, coaching and help," she said. "But there has long been a culture in the child-serving agencies in Maryland that disregards the autonomy, the dignity and the voices of youth."<br/><br/>Egan said she hopes the training contributes to a culture shift inside the department from harsh, sometimes arbitrary punishment to true rehabilitation.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>She questioned why the training isn't being given to DJS staff in detention centers. A spokesman for the department cited limited resources and said those facilities have mental and behavioral health professionals.<br/><br/>Tough questions<br/><br/>Inside the Roca Baltimore office on a recent afternoon, about a dozen young men wrote down some of their deepest concerns and most pressing questions, then crumpled up the anonymous responses and threw them into a bucket.<br/><br/>Academic and life skills instructor Zoe Andrade picked some at random and read them aloud so the young men could offer advice. Their answers contained nuggets of CBT wisdom, profound statements interspersed with sometimes irreverent jokes.<br/><br/>One participant wrote he was "in a confusing place," wondering whether he should "let my brother rest in peace or retaliate."<br/><br/>Jonathan Holloway, 23, offered a response based on personal experience; his brother also had been shot.<br/><br/>"You've gotta start living your own life," he said. "I still want to retaliate, but I'm trying to better myself. I feel like everything I'm doing at Roca would be for nothing."<br/><br/>The group also considered two questions about whether to quit Roca's job training program and go make more money in the streets.<br/><br/>"The block is doing numbers right now. Should I go back out?" one participant asked. Holloway spoke up again, challenging his peers to think about the risks of ending up dead or locked up.<br/><br/>A question about relationship drama — one young man said he found a woman slashing his car's tires that morning — produced consensus on letting karma take care of it. A discussion about the importance of hard work and consistency included a metaphor about turning dirt into diamonds, the message being that hard-earned cash comes with a stronger sense of accomplishment.<br/><br/>"If you want something you never had, you've gotta do things you've never done," said Louis Pearl, 21. "Manifest the things you want."<br/><br/>Keon Vines described the satisfaction of proving people wrong. During a recent stint behind bars, he told a friend he planned to "come home and chill, get a job or something" upon his release. The friend didn't believe him.<br/><br/>"But look at me now," said Vines, breaking into a triumphant smile. It was the day before his 20th birthday, and Vines found himself finally feeling optimistic about his future and surrounded by people who wanted to help him succeed.<br/><br/>Advertisement<br/><br/>The room erupted in cheers; his joy was contagious.<br/><br/>Paul Finley, employment specialist with Roca Baltimore, speaks to young men in the program. Staff members use cognitive behavioral therapy to help the young men change their thought patterns and behaviors. (Kim Hairston/Baltimore Sun ) | Stórálann an suíomh Gréasáin seo sonraí mar fhianáin chun feidhmiúlacht riachtanach an láithreáin a chumasú, chomh maith le margaíocht, pearsantú agus anailísíocht.Trí do thoiliú a bheith ar an suíomh Gréasáin seo, cuireann tú in iúl.<br/><br/>'Féach ar dom anois': Ag baint úsáide as an néaróchas chun cuidiú le páistí atá i mbaol — agus athrú ar chóras ceartais inmhaí<br/><br/>Go raibh maith agat as tacú lenár n-iriseoir. Tá an t-alt seo ar fáil go heisiach dár síntiúsóirí, a chuidíonn lenár gcuid oibre a mhaoiniú ag an Baltimore Sun.<br/><br/>Íomhá 1 de 9<br/><br/>Labhraíonn Paul Finley, speisialtóir fostaíochta le fir óga sa chlár, agus oibríonn foireann na Rosa a bhfuil baint acu leis an gcóras ceartais ag baint úsáide as CBT, teiripe iompraíochta cognaíocha, chun cabhrú leo a bpatrúin smaointeoireachta agus a n-iompraíochta a athrú. (Kim Hairston / Baltimmore Sun)<br/><br/>Bhí Raynold Smith ag beith le fear eile ar feadh míonna agus nuair a thrasnaigh siad cosáin i Márta 2021, armtha an bheirt acu.<br/><br/>An chúis nár tharraing Smith an truicir? I nóiméad scoilt-dara, nuair a chuaigh an saol agus bás san iarmhéid, ghleoite sé suíochán carr leanaí agus thuig sé go tobann go raibh gach rud a namhaid a chailleadh. Beagnach láithreach, bhraith Smith sracadh piléar trína chos, ag iarraidh go caolaigh ar mhór-rannóg agus a iomródh sé ar feadh na seachtaine.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Ba é sin an dara huair a bhí Smith, 26, Baltimore, lámhaigh; d'fhág lámhach 2019 é le créachtaí graze. Bhí a fhios aige go raibh rud éigin le hathrú.<br/><br/>Sna míonna amach romhainn, fuair sé amach cad a bhí ag teastáil uaidh i Rosca, clár neamhbhrabúis frith-foréigean, i Baltimore. Chomh maith le ranganna oiliúna agus scileanna poist, cabhraíonn an clár le déagóirí agus fir óga teacht chucu féin agus iad ag iarraidh cosán nua a chruthú – trína gcuid brains a athscríobh.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Chuige sin, úsáideann Rosa an méid a iarrann sé teiripe iompraíochta cognaíocha, rud a dhíríonn ar chaidreamh smaointe, mothúchán agus gníomhartha a scrúdú.Tá an teoiric réasúnta simplí, ach is féidir na torthaí a bheith as cuimse, de réir fhoireann an chláir agus rannpháirtithe.<br/><br/>An bhféadfadh méadú ar úsáid CBT i measc na hóige leochaileacha cabhrú le foréigean an ghunna a laghdú agus pobail níos sláintiúla, níos athléimní a chruthú? Tá saineolaithe agus oifigigh dóchasach, agus tá sé beartaithe ag Roinn Sheirbhísí Ógánach, i gcomhpháirtíocht le Rosca, fáil amach.<br/><br/>Calvin Monroe, d'fhág, oibrithe óige Roca Baltimore, barróg Raynold Smith, 26, tar éis dóibh seiceáil isteach leis.Oibríonn baill foirne Rica le fir óga a bhfuil baint acu leis an gcóras ceartais ag baint úsáide as teiripe iompraíochta cognaíocha. Beidh an Rosca ag traenáil in aghaidh bhaill foirne de chuid na Roinne Seirbhísí Óghílse i CBT chun úsáid a bhaint as na páistí sa chóras ceartais faoi úinéireacht áitiúil (Kim Hairston/Baltimore Sun)<br/><br/>Níos luaithe i mbliana, d’fhógair ceannairí na roinne go bhfaigheadh 300 ball foirne – lena n-áirítear go leor daoine óga a oibríonn ar phromhadh fíonghoirt nó maoirseacht iar-eisiúint – oiliúint ó Mharacó ar eolaíocht na hógánache inchinn, síceolaíocht na tráma agus CBT.<br/><br/>Íocfaidh deontas cónaidhme beagnach $ 1 mhilliún as an oiliúint, a thagann i measc bhrú forleathan le haghaidh athchóiriú ceartais faoi aois. Rith an Tionól Ginearálta sraith billí i mbliana leis an sprioc sin, lena n-áirítear deireadh a chur le gaibhniú óige ar feadh na mí-aoiseanna is mó a dhéantar den chéad uair, agus leagann sé síos íoscheanglais aoise do mhuirir choiriúla agus chuir sé teorainn le fad na dtéarmaí promhaidh.<br/><br/>Tá go leor de ghortú agus pian ag Baltimore," a dúirt Ronaldtea Alexander, maoirseoir cás-sheirbhíse a chríochnaigh an oiliúint le déanaí. "Spreagann sé seo dúinn dul isteach agus cabhrú leis na teaghlaigh seo. Osclaíonn sé an doras chun iad a thaispeáint go bhfuil rogha difriúil ann."<br/><br/>Chloígh cinneadh an dara ceann trua trua trua leis na scileanna atá aige ó shin solided., Shíl sé mar gheall ar na hiarmhairtí a d'fhéadfadh a bheith ann - leanbh gafa sa chros tine - agus ní raibh shoot. Anois, tuigeann sé é i gcomhthéacs ceann de na tiontáin CBT: "Gníomh ar do luachanna."<br/><br/>Chuir sé i bhfeidhm le déanaí é i staid eile so-ghalaithe., amhrasta sé infidelity i gcaidreamh, fuair feargach agus bhí claonta i dtreo foréigin. Ansin mheas sé go léir a bhí á chailleadh: a shaoirse, a chuid páistí, a dhá phost. Leis an teanga a chur in iúl a chinneadh agus córas tacaíochta, bhí sé níos éasca dul ar shiúl an uair seo: "Ní fiú roinnt rudaí," a dúirt sé, shrruging.<br/><br/>Ina áit sin, phioc sé suas níos mó athruithe, go minic ag obair seacht lá na seachtaine idir roinn loingseoireachta na cuideachta grafaicí i Timonium agus mar rádala bia ag an Baltimore Comedy Factory.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Raynold Smith, ar chlé, agus Calvin Monroe, oibrí óige Roca Baltimore, labhair faoi shaincheisteanna a bhfuil Smith ag déileáil leo. Oibríonn baill foirne na nGardaí le fir óga a bhfuil baint acu leis an gcóras ceartais ag baint úsáide as teiripe iompraíochta cognaíocha, nó CBT, chun cabhrú leo a bpatrúin smaointeoireachta agus a n-iompraíochta a athrú.<br/><br/>Dúirt Smith go gcreideann sé gur chuir oifigeach póilíní nó oibrí sóisialta é faoi bhráid Rocka tar éis dó bualadh leis san ospidéal tar éis dó lámhaigh a fháil anuraidh.<br/><br/>Trí CBT agus a dhlúthchaidreamh le Calvin Monroe, a shanntar d'oibrí na gcarrae, chuir Smith an clár i gcrích agus a choinneáil socair agus a chothromú. Dúirt Smith a chuid mothúchán go fóill go ligeann sé dó gníomhartha impulsive a sheachaint a d’fhéadfadh sé a bheith aiféala.<br/><br/>Buan lasmuigh dá choimpléasc árasán le linn seiceála isteach le déanaí le Monroe, chuaigh Smith faoi bheith ina dhuine tí: chora a dhéanamh agus fanacht sábháilte.<br/><br/>Ina theannta sin, is dúshlán ollmhór é fir óga na sráideanna a fhágáil – nuair is minic a sháraíonn gealltanas airgid tapa an baol foréigin – agus an chobhsaíocht fhadtéarmach a roghnú, fiú amháin más rud é go gciallaíonn sé sin go bhfuil íosphá nó go bhfuil orthu ranganna ardmhinicíochta comhionannais scoile a ghlacadh.<br/><br/>Tá plean scoir ar bith ar na sráideanna.Dúirt Monroe: “sin cad a choinníonn mé iad.”<br/><br/>Athruithe san inchinn<br/><br/>Díríonn an clár a d’fhorbair Roca ar thimthriall "Tink-Meithe-A dhéanamh" a aithint agus cur isteach orthu chun torthaí diúltacha féideartha a sheachaint.Ó dhearcadh néareolaíoch, ciallaíonn sé sin go minic cosáin nua a chruthú san inchinn agus iad a neartú le himeacht ama.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Bunaithe i Massachusetts níos mó ná 30 bliain ó shin, d'oscail Rocco a oifig Baltimore i 2018. Tá cáil air as rath le cuid de na fir óga is buartha agus a d'fhéadfadh a bheith contúirteach.<br/><br/>Múineann an clár seacht scil chun cur isteach ar timthriallta míshláintiúla.Is é an chéad cheann ná "Bí i láthair," in ionad baill foirne a shocrú ar an am atá caite nó amach anseo, dúirt baill foirne eile.Áirítear ar "Dochar do chuid mothúchán", "bata in éineacht leis" agus "Flex do smaointeoireacht."<br/><br/>Deir saineolaithe gur féidir leis an gcineál seo teiripe a bheith tairbheach do dhaoine atá ag téarnamh ó thráma, toisc go gcaitheann siad níos mó ama i mód "troid nó eitilt".<br/><br/>Nuair a bhíonn tráma ag daoine go minic – cosúil le foréigean gunna a fheiceáil go rialta – a n-athruithe ar ghníomhaíocht inchinn chun tuiscint níos airde a léiriú ar chontúirt. Go gcruthaíonn sé sin gníomhaíocht níos mó sa amygda, an réigiún a bhaineann le freagraí eagla agus strus, agus níos lú sa cortex tosaigh réamhlíne.Sé sin nuair a chabhraíonn réasúnaíocht le mothúcháin agus impulses a rialú, rud a fhágann go bhfuil cinnteoireacht níos cúramach. I gcás fhormhór na ndaoine, is é an cortex tosaigh is faide a fhorbairt, a bhaint amach aibíocht timpeall 25 bliana.<br/><br/>Le linn cruinniú mullaigh a d'óstáil Scoil Leighis Ollscoil Maryland i Baltimore, dúirt an Méara Bradon Scott gur sheinn sé duine éigin den chéad uair.<br/><br/>Ag fás aníos óg agus Dubh in Ards Pháirc, ina gcónaí le trám an fhoréigin gunna - bhí a fhios ag gach duine go raibh an taithí chéanna aige. Shíl muid go raibh sé gnáth," a dúirt sé. "Ní mór dúinn smaoineamh i ndáiríre ar an gcaoi a dtéann duine i bhfeidhm ar inchinn."<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Dúirt an Dr. Kerry Resler, ollamh le síciatraí i Scoil Leighis Harvard, go bhfuil rátaí iar-thubaill i roinnt chomharsanachtaí uirbeacha ná i measc veterans míleata.<br/><br/>"Ó thaobh na síneireachta, tá daoine i ndáiríre ag maireachtáil i gcriosanna cogaidh," a dúirt sé ag an gcruinniú mullaigh. "Tá daoine ag éirí i dtrioblóid agus ag cur le timthriallta foréigin i bpáirt mar gheall ar tráma gan chóireáil."<br/><br/>Is féidir le cóireálacha cosúil le CBT athruithe intomhaiste a dhéanamh ar ghníomhaíocht inchinne a chuireann torthaí níos sláintiúla chun cinn, a dúirt sé.<br/><br/>Tugann sé seo cothromas mothúchánach dóibh'<br/><br/>I Roinn Mary de Sheirbhísí Ógánach, ba iad baill foirne i Baltimore an chéad duine a chuaigh faoi oiliúint Rewire Rosca; sa deireadh, leathnóidh sé an stát.<br/><br/>Bhí amhras ar chuid acu go n-aistreofaí clár oiliúna 11 seachtaine ar theoiric shíceolaíoch go mbeadh idirghníomhaíochtaí feabhsaithe acu leis na leanaí a dhéanann siad faoi mhaoirseacht. Ach ag pointe éigin, chuaigh an bolgán solais amach do Justine Buckingham, maoirseoir bainisteoir cás seirbhísí jungle.<br/><br/>Anois, tarraingíonn sí amach bileoga oibre go minic chun cabhrú lena cliaint smaointe, mothúcháin agus gníomhartha idirnasctha a iniúchadh. Mar shampla, chuir sí in iúl do léaráid ag fear óg a raibh fadhbanna aige ar scoil. Ag smaoineamh nach raibh a fhios aige go leor chun pas a fháil i tástáil a rinneadh é bhraitheann neirbhíseach agus díomá, a thug air an scoil a scipeáil agus dul i dtrioblóid.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Ag aithint gur cheadaigh an timthriall sin dó toradh eile a shamhlú, dúirt Buckingham. Cad a d'fhoghlaim sé dá mba rud é go raibh sé bródúil as a chuid ranganna a rith? Ansin, d'fhéadfadh sé a bheith bródúil as, fanacht ar scoil agus a dioplómaí a thuilleamh.<br/><br/>Tá daoine óga cuntasach ar an mbealach seo, dúirt sí, seachas cloí le horduithe breitheamh.<br/><br/>Dúradh leis na páistí seo an oiread sin faoi cé hiad féin, cad a thiocfaidh siad chun bheith nó nach mbeidh. Ach ní thugtar léarscáil bhóithre dóibh riamh," a dúirt James "JT" Timpson, stiúrthóir comhpháirtíochtaí pobail ag Romaigh. "Tugann sé seo cothromas mhothúchánach dóibh. Tugann sé smacht dóibh gan cuntasacht a chur ar shiúl."<br/><br/>Dúirt Jenny Egan, a dhéanann maoirseacht ar rannán óg Baltimore d'Oifig an GCosantóirí Poiblí, go bhfuil an tionscnamh thar téarma cé go bhfuil sí faoi dhíospóid, cé gur chóir é a lipéadú teiripe iompraíochta cognaíocha, téarma cliniciúil a thagraíonn do chineál cóireála síceolaíoch. Mar sin féin, dúirt sí gur an chéad chéim é an cur chuige bunaithe ar fhianaise chun torthaí a fheabhsú d’óige leochaileacha.<br/><br/>Ach tá cultúr ar fáil sna gníomhaireachtaí a fhreastalaíonn ar leanaí i Maryland a thugann neamhaird ar neamhspleáchas, dínit agus guthanna na hóige. "Iarrtar ar an gcóras seo a bheith ag tairiscint na bpáistí, is é sin treoir, cóitseáil agus cabhair a thabhairt di."<br/><br/>Egan dúirt sé go bhfuil súil aici go gcuirfidh an oiliúint le hathrú cultúr taobh istigh den roinn ó chrua, uaireanta pionós treallach ar fhíor-athshlánú.<br/><br/>Fógraíocht<br/><br/>Cheistigh sí cén fáth nach bhfuil an oiliúint á tabhairt do bhaill foirne DJS in ionaid coinneála. Labhairadóir don roinn chuirtí teoranta acmhainní ar fáil agus dúirt sí go bhfuil gairmithe meabhairshláinte agus iompraíochta ag na saoráidí sin.<br/><br/>Ceisteanna diana<br/><br/>Taobh istigh den oifig Rosa Baltimore ag tráthnóna le déanaí, scríobh thart ar fhear óg dosaen síos cuid dá n-imní is doimhne agus den chuid is mó ag brú ceisteanna, agus ansin lean siad suas na freagraí gan ainm agus chaith siad isteach i buicéad.<br/><br/>Ghlac an teagascóir acadúil agus saoil Zoe Andade cuid acu go randamach agus léigh siad os ard iad ionas go bhféadfadh na fir óga a gcuid freagraí a thabhairt ar na ráitis go bhfuil eagna CBT iontu, agus iad á léiriú le scéalta grinn a bhí gan cuimhneamh uaireanta.<br/><br/>Bhí duine amháin a scríobh bhí sé "in áit mearbhall," wondering ar chóir dó "lig mo dheartháir scíth i síocháin nó i gcoibhneas."<br/><br/>Thug Jonathan Holloway, 23, toradh bunaithe ar thaithí phearsanta; scaoileadh a dheartháir é freisin.<br/><br/>Tá tú gotta tús a chónaí do shaol féin," a dúirt sé. "Ba mhaith liom fós a rá, ach tá mé ag iarraidh a bheith níos fearr dom féin., Is dóigh liom go mbeadh gach rud ag déanamh mé ag Roma mhaith a bheith ar rud ar bith."<br/><br/>Rinne an grúpa dhá cheist freisin faoi cé acu a chaithfidh tú clár oiliúna poist Rosca a scor agus níos mó airgid a dhéanamh ar na sráideanna.<br/><br/>Tá an bloc ag déanamh uimhreacha ceart anois. Ar chóir dom dul ar ais amach?" labhair rannpháirtí amháin le Holloway suas arís, ag tabhairt dúshlán dá chomh bpiaraí smaoineamh ar na rioscaí a bhaineann le deireadh a chur le marbh nó le daoine faoi ghlas.<br/><br/>Ceist faoi dhráma caidrimh – fear óg amháin a dúirt gur fuair sé bean a bhí ag slais boinn carr a bhí ar maidin – thug sé comhdhearcadh maidir le karma a ligean aire a thabhairt dó. I measc na díospóireachta faoi thábhacht na hoibre crua agus an chomhsheasmhacht bhí meafar le meafarr faoi chasadh an salachar ar diamonds, is é an teachtaireacht go dtagann airgead tirim crua-thuillte le tuiscint níos láidre a bhaint amach.<br/><br/>"Más mian leat rud éigin riamh go raibh tú, tá tú gotta rudaí a rinne tú riamh," a dúirt Louis Pearl, 21. "Malaest na rudaí is mian leat."<br/><br/>Chuir Keon Víves síos ar an sásamh a bhain le daoine a chruthú mícheart. | Herbal teas have been consumed for centuries for their numerous health benefits. Packed with natural ingredients and essential nutrients, these delightful beverages offer a refreshing way to promote optimal health. In this article, we delve into the power of herbal teas and explore their potential to enhance overall well-being. Discover the wonders of herbal teas and how they can contribute to a healthier lifestyle.<br/><br/>The Benefits of Herbal Teas for Physical Health: Herbal teas are renowned for their ability to support physical well-being. Their antioxidant properties help combat free radicals and reduce oxidative stress, which may lead to various health issues. Moreover, certain herbal teas, such as chamomile and peppermint, are known for their soothing effects on the digestive system. Including herbal teas in your daily routine can promote a healthy gut, aid digestion, and alleviate common gastrointestinal discomfort.<br/><br/>Boosting Mental Wellness with Herbal Teas: In addition to physical health, herbal teas can also have a positive impact on mental well-being. Many herbal teas possess calming properties that can help reduce anxiety and stress. Popular choices such as lavender and lemon balm are known for their relaxing effects, promoting a sense of calmness and tranquility. By incorporating herbal teas into your daily routine, you can create a soothing ritual that promotes mental clarity and emotional balance.<br/><br/>Herbal Teas as Natural Remedies: Herbal teas have long been used as natural remedies for various ailments. With their healing properties, they offer a gentle and holistic approach to wellness. For instance, ginger tea is often consumed to alleviate nausea and aid digestion. Echinacea tea is popular for boosting the immune system, while elderberry tea is believed to provide relief from cold and flu symptoms. By harnessing the power of nature, herbal teas offer a natural alternative to conventional medicines.<br/><br/>Herbal Teas for Detoxification: Detoxifying the body is essential for optimal health, and herbal teas can play a vital role in this process. Certain herbal teas, such as dandelion and nettle tea, are known for their diuretic properties, aiding in the elimination of toxins and waste from the body. Additionally, herbal teas like green tea and milk thistle tea support liver health, which is crucial for effective detoxification. By incorporating detoxifying herbal teas into your wellness routine, you can support your body's natural cleansing processes.<br/><br/>Herbal Teas for Sleep and Relaxation: In today's fast-paced world, getting quality sleep is essential for overall well-being. Herbal teas can be a valuable tool for promoting restful sleep and relaxation. Chamomile tea, with its mild sedative properties, has been used for centuries to improve sleep quality. Valerian root tea and passionflower tea are also known for their calming effects, helping to ease insomnia and promote a deeper, more restorative sleep. By sipping on a soothing herbal tea before bed, you can create a peaceful bedtime routine and improve your sleep patterns.<br/><br/>Incorporating Herbal Teas into Your Daily Routine: Now that you are aware of the myriad benefits of herbal teas, it's time to explore ways to incorporate them into your daily routine. Start by selecting a variety of herbal teas that cater to your specific health needs and personal preferences. Experiment with different flavors and blends to find the ones you enjoy the most. Consider replacing sugary or caffeinated beverages with herbal teas for a healthier alternative. Remember to brew your herbal tea correctly to ensure you extract the maximum benefits from the herbs.<br/><br/>Conclusion: Herbal teas offer a delightful and effective way to enhance your overall health and well-being. From supporting physical health and mental wellness to providing natural remedies and promoting detoxification, herbal teas are a treasure trove of health benefits. By including these herbal concoctions in your daily routine, you can embark on a journey toward optimal health. So, explore the power of herbal teas and unlock their potential for a healthier and happier you | Tá tae luibhe caite le haghaidh na gcéadta bliain ar mhaithe lena gcuid buntáistí sláinte iomadúla. Pacáilte le comhábhair nádúrtha agus cothaithigh riachtanacha, cuireann na deochanna blasta seo bealach athnuachana ar fáil chun an tsláinte is fearr is féidir a chur chun cinn. San Airteagal seo, déanaimid iniúchadh ar chumhacht na dtábhrach luibhe agus déanfaimid iniúchadh ar a n-acmhainn chun folláine iomlán a fheabhsú.Faigh amach iontais na dtáise luibhe agus conas is féidir leo cur le stíl mhaireachtála níos sláintiúla.<br/><br/>Na Buntáistí a bhaineann le Teas luibhe le Sláinte Fhisiciúil: Tá cáil ar thaithí luibhe as a gcumas tacú le folláine fhisiceach. Cuidíonn a n-airíonna antioxidant chun fréamhacha saor in aisce a chomhrac agus strus ocsaídiúcháin a laghdú, rud a d’fhéadfadh saincheisteanna sláinte éagsúla a bheith mar thoradh air. Thairis sin, tá tae luibhe áirithe, mar shampla chamomile agus lus an phiobair, ar eolas mar gheall ar a n-éifeachtaí soothing ar an gcóras díleá. Lena n-áirítear tae luibhe i do ghnáthamh laethúil is féidir a chur chun cinn gut sláintiúil, díleá cabhrach, agus míchompord gastrointestinal coiteann a mhaolú.<br/><br/>Folláine Meabhair-Ghalar a threisiú le Séasúir Luibhe: Chomh maith leis an tsláinte fhisiceach, is féidir tionchar dearfach a bheith ag tae luibhe ar fholláine mheabhrach.Tá go leor airíonna ceansaithe ag tae luibhe a chabhróidh le himní agus strus a laghdú. Tá roghanna coitianta ar nós lavender agus balm líomóide ar eolas mar gheall ar a n-éifeachtaí scíth a ligean, tuiscint ar shochla agus suaimhneas a chur chun cinn. Trí fhírinní luibhe a ionchorprú i do ghnáthamh laethúil, is féidir leat dóiteán soothing a chuireann soiléireacht mheabhrach agus cothromaíocht mhothúchánach a chruthú.<br/><br/>Teas luibhe mar Leigheasanna Nádúrtha: Úsáideadh tae luibhe le fada mar leigheasanna nádúrtha le haghaidh tinnis éagsúla.Leis an airíonna cneasaithe a bhí acu, tairgeann siad cur chuige milis agus iomlánaíoch maidir le folláine. Mar shampla, is minic a chaitear tae ginger chun nausea agus díleá cabhrach a mhaolú.Tá an-tóir ar Epighlaca chun an córas imdhíonachta a threisiú, agus creidtear go gcuireann tae elder faoiseamh ó comharthaí fuar agus fliú. Trí leas a bhaint as cumhacht an nádúir, cuireann tae luibhe rogha nádúrtha ar fáil seachas gnáth-mhíochaine.<br/><br/>Teas luibhe le haghaidh Dí-chocsainiú: Tá díthocsainiú ar an gcomhlacht riachtanach don tsláinte is fearr, agus is féidir le tae luibhe ról ríthábhachtach a bheith acu sa phróiseas seo. Tá tae luibhe áirithe, mar shampla dandelion agus tae nettle, ar eolas mar gheall ar a n-airíonna uafásacha, ag cabhrú le deireadh a chur le tocsainí agus dramhaíl ón gcomhlacht. Ina theannta sin, tacaíonn tae luibhe le sláinte ae agus tae feadaíl glas a fháil, rud atá ríthábhachtach le haghaidh díthocsainiú éifeachtach.Trí thacaí luibhe a ionchorprú i do ghnáthamh folláine, is féidir leat tacú le próisis glantacháin nádúrtha do choirp.<br/><br/>Teas luibhe le haghaidh codlata agus scíthe: I ndomhan an lae inniu, tá sé riachtanach codladh ardchaighdeáin a fháil chun folláine iomlán a chur chun cinn.Is uirlis luachmhar é tae luibhe chun codladh agus scíthe a chur ar aghaidh. Baineadh úsáid as tae chamomile, lena airíonna síoga éadroma, ar feadh na gcéadta bliain chun cáilíocht codlata a fheabhsú.Tá tae fréimhe Valerian agus tae paisean ar eolas freisin as a n-éifeachtaí suaimhneacha, ag cabhrú le insomnia a mhaolú agus codladh níos doimhne, níos aisiríoch a chur chun cinn. Trí sleamhnú ar tae luibhe soothing roimh leaba, is féidir leat a chruthú ghnáthamh am codlata síochánta agus do phatrúin codlata a fheabhsú.<br/><br/>A chuimsíonn Teas luibhe isteach i do Ráithín Lae Lae: Anois go bhfuil tú ar an eolas faoi na buntáistí iomadúla a bhaineann le tae luibhe, tá sé in am bealaí a iniúchadh chun iad a ionchorprú i do ghnáthamh laethúil. Tosaigh trí thaes luibhe éagsúla a roghnú a fhreastalaíonn ar do riachtanais sláinte ar leith agus do roghanna pearsanta. Turgnamh le blasanna agus cumaisc éagsúla chun na cinn is mó a thaitníonn leat a fháil. Déan machnamh ar deochanna siúcra nó caiféin le tae luibhe le haghaidh rogha níos sláintiúla. Cuimhnigh a dhéanamh i gceart do tae luibhe chun na buntáistí is mó a bhaint as na luibheanna.<br/><br/>Conclúid: Tairgeann tae luibhe bealach iontach éifeachtach chun do shláinte agus folláine iomlán a fheabhsú. Ó thacaíocht a thabhairt do shláinte fhisiciúil agus mheabhrach leigheasanna nádúrtha a sholáthar agus díthocsainiú a chur chun cinn, is taisce de shochair sláinte iad tae luibhe. Trí na naisc luibhe seo a áireamh i do ghnáthamh laethúil, is féidir leat dul ar thuras i dtreo na sláinte is fearr is féidir.Mar sin, iniúchadh a dhéanamh ar chumhacht na dteataí luibhe agus an acmhainneacht atá acu do shláinte níos sláintiúla agus níos sona a bhaint amach |
| Things To Consider For Protecting The Exterior Of Your House<br/><br/>It's easy to fix interior tasks such as maintaining your air-conditioners, painting your living rooms, fixing leaking taps and faucets, etc. These tasks are easy to monitor because their associated problems are all the time in front of us.<br/><br/>Most people can do it on their own, but there is no shame in seeking out a professional's help too. After all, your home's safety comes first, and thus, just handling the interior isn't enough! But how do we fix our exteriors? What all can we do to ensure that our boundary walls remain strong and beautiful?<br/><br/>This article takes you through some basic steps in keeping our exteriors strong and well-maintained.<br/><br/>Prune away your surrounding trees, grass, plants, etc. Fallen branches and leaves can threaten your walls and foundations in more ways than one. Decaying leaves and branches secrete acids and other fluids that can damage the foundations of your walls. While having greenery around us is desirable, it is equally important to keep trees and shrubs at bay.<br/><br/>Watch out for the roots of the surrounding trees. If you aren't watchful, these roots might creep in and destroy the foundations of your house. Similarly, don't let grass and small plants grow on your walls. Please remove them in the first instance.<br/><br/>Fix your cracks. Since your house is made up of concrete, it may develop cracks over time. Fix these cracks as soon as you see them. Don't sleep over the job; plug those cracks at the first instance. If you ignore these tiny cracks, these will become bigger, and the problem would become unmanageable.<br/><br/>To fix these small cracks, you may consult specialists like Rekote.<br/><br/>Paint your exteriors once in every three years. Your outer walls are subject to rain, snow, and sun all the time. Not surprisingly, they may fall prey very soon if you aren't careful. Protect your exteriors by painting them with appropriate colors. For an excellent painting job, you will have to prepare your walls. Scrape the unwanted chemicals and materials off, and then apply a primer. Leave the walls for some time, and then use a fresh coat of paint. Keep an eye on the moisture in the wall. If you aren't careful, this moisture might erode the paint a few years from now.<br/><br/>Check your roof. Look out for damaged, curled, bald shingles. If your shingles are curled up or have gone bald, it is time to re-do your roof. Curled up shingles mean that your roof has lost its strength. Similarly, look out for missing shingles. This means that your roof is directly exposed to sun, snow, and water. Check whether there is any moss on your roof. Sprouting of moss means possible decay of your roof-materials. Remove this moss with the help of water and specialized chemicals.<br/><br/>Clean up your main door. Remove dust, and stains from your exterior door. Repaint it periodically. Please don't use an abrasive while cleaning it; else your door would look ugly and spotted. Similarly, clean up your windows; remove any stains on the outside glass with the usage of the right chemicals.<br/><br/>Clean up the gutters. Check whether any small branches, grass or any other objects are clogging your gutters. If the covers of your gutters are damaged, replace them with new ones. Cleaning up gutters and drain pipes is very important for keeping your house hygienic. Call an expert if the problem becomes serious.<br/><br/>Effective weatherstripping of your doors and windows; Check whether your doors and windows are weather-proof. This is important to make your home warm and comfortable. Replace the older weatherstripping if there is a need for it.<br/><br/>Repair window gaps regularly. Plug them with sealants so that your home is secure and warm. | Rudaí le Smaoineamh Chun Taobh seachtrach de do Theach a Chosaint<br/><br/>Is furasta tascanna istigh a shocrú mar do aer-chóiritheoirí a chothabháil, do sheomraí maireachtála a phéinteáil, sconnaí agus faucets sceitheadh a shocrú, etc Is furasta na tascanna seo a dhéanamh toisc go bhfuil a gcuid fadhbanna gaolmhara an t-am ar fad os ár gcomhair.<br/><br/>Is féidir le formhór na ndaoine é a dhéanamh leo féin, ach níl aon náire ann cabhair ghairmiúil a lorg freisin.Tar éis an tsaoil, tagann sábháilteacht do theach ar dtús, agus dá bhrí sin, níl mórán láimhseáil ar an taobh istigh! Ach conas a shocraigh muid ár taobh amuigh? Cad is féidir linn a dhéanamh chun a chinntiú go bhfanann ár ballaí teorann láidir agus álainn?<br/><br/>Tógann an t-alt seo tú trí roinnt céimeanna bunúsacha chun ár taobh amuigh a choinneáil láidir agus dea-choimeádta.<br/><br/>Sruthanna agus duilleoga ag éalú ó do chrainn máguaird, féir, plandaí, etc. Is féidir le craobhacha agus duilleoga tar éis titim do ballaí agus do fhondúireachtaí a bhagairt ar níos mó ná bealach amháin. Cé go bhfuil fuinneamh againn atá inmhianaithe, tá sé chomh tábhachtach céanna crainn agus toir a choinneáil ar bhá.<br/><br/>Bí ag faire amach do fréamhacha na gcrann máguaird.Mura bhfuil tú watchful, d'fhéadfadh na fréamhacha seo bunús do theach a creep isteach agus scrios.Mar an gcéanna, ná lig féar agus plandaí beaga ag fás ar do bhallaí. Bain iad ar an gcéad dul síos.<br/><br/>D'eisigh do charr.Ós rud é go bhfuil do theach déanta suas de coincréite, d'fhéadfadh sé scoilteanna a fhorbairt le himeacht ama. D'eisigh na scoilteanna seo chomh luath agus a fheiceann tú iad. Ná codladh thar an bpost; Má dhéanann tú neamhaird ar na scoilteanna beag bídeach seo, éireoidh siad seo níos mó, agus ní bheadh an fhadhb do-bhainistithe.<br/><br/>Chun na scoilteanna beaga seo a shocrú, féadfaidh tú dul i gcomhairle le speisialtóirí cosúil le Rekote.<br/><br/>Péint do taobh amuigh uair amháin i ngach trí bliana. Tá do ballaí seachtracha faoi réir báisteach, sneachta agus gréine an t-am ar fad., Ní ionadh, d'fhéadfadh siad titim chreiche go han-luath más rud é nach bhfuil tú cúramach. do taobh amuigh ag péinteáil leo le dathanna cuí. Chun post péintéireachta den scoth, beidh ort a ullmhú do bhallaí. Scrap na ceimiceáin agus na hábhair nach dteastaíonn uait, agus ansin iarratas a dhéanamh ar primer.Fág na ballaí ar feadh tamaill, agus ansin bain úsáid as cóta úr péint.Coinnigh súil ar an taise sa bhalla. Mura bhfuil tú cúramach, d'fhéadfadh an taise seo rode an péint cúpla bliain ó anois.<br/><br/>Seiceáil do dhíon.Fuath amach le haghaidh damáiste, cuachta, shingles maol.Má tá do shingles cuachta suas nó má imithe maol, tá sé in am do díon a ath-roisneadh.Ciallaíonn gearrthóirí suas go bhfuil do dhíon caillte a neart.Mar an gcéanna, féach ar shileoga ar iarraidh. Ciallaíonn sé seo go bhfuil do dhíon nochtaithe go díreach do ghrian, sneachta agus uisce.Seiceáil an bhfuil aon mhín ar do dhíon.Braitheann sporadh caon lobhadh ar do chuid ábhar díon.Bain an caonach le cabhair uisce agus ceimiceáin speisialaithe.<br/><br/>Glan suas do phríomhdhora.Bain deannach, agus stains ó do dhoras taobh amuigh.Repaint go tréimhsiúil.Ná húsáid scríobach le linn é a ghlanadh; eile bheadh do doras cuma ghránna agus chonaic. Ar an gcaoi chéanna, glan do chuid fuinneoga; bain aon stains ar an ghloine lasmuigh le húsáid na gceimiceán ceart.<br/><br/>Déan seiceáil an bhfuil aon cheann de na craobhacha beaga, féar nó aon rudaí eile ag clogging do ghodóirí.Má dhéantar damáiste do chumhdach do ghoitéar, cuir ceann nua ina n-áit. Tá sé an-tábhachtach do ghoitéirí agus píopaí draein a ghlanadh chun do theach a choinneáil sláinteachais. Glaoigh ar shaineolaí má bhíonn an fhadhb tromchúiseach.<br/><br/>Tá sé seo tábhachtach do theach a dhéanamh te agus compordach. Cuir an aimsir níos sine in ionad anála, má tá gá leis. Déan seiceáil an bhfuil do chuid doirse agus fuinneoga fút féin, déan seiceáil an bhfuil an aimsir aimsir bhriontach te agus compordach.<br/><br/>bearnaí fuinneoige a dheisiú go rialta.Cuir isteach iad le séalaí ionas go mbeidh do theach slán agus te. |

| Causes of Yellow Teeth & 9 Home Remedies for Teeth Whitening<br/><br/>Smile is the strongest way to attract anyone towards you and this is the way to look you more attractive. But if you have the poor color of teeth than you feel embarrassing in front of anybody. Yellow teeth put a bad impact on your personality and you avoid to smile anywhere. The discoloration of teeth slowly exists and you might not take it seriously but by the time your teeth turned to white and decreased your self-confidence.<br/><br/>The discoloration of teeth is not a big serious problem but it decreases your confident level in front of people. There are many reasons of teeth discoloration but one of the main reason is the food we eat. If intake of food is not good; that is we take more artificial food and not the natural one then it will turn our teeth to yellow.<br/><br/>The artificial colors in food stains our teeth and ultimately by the passage of time our teeth becomes yellow. Drinking harmful beverages like soda and tea also plays an important role in teeth discoloration because high content of soda damage protective layer of teeth and results to decay enamel coating.<br/><br/>Credit: Health Insider<br/><br/>The other main reason for yellow teeth is not caring your personal hygiene and not brushing it regularly. Age factor and hereditary conditions also a main reason in discoloration.<br/><br/>You can minimize this problem by quitting those foods that cause teeth discoloration. Some of them are mentioned below.<br/><br/>What Causes Yellow Teeth?<br/><br/>1. Cola, Soda and Sports Drinks:<br/><br/>Drinks having alcohol and caffeine damage the natural enamel. Excessive use of black tea and coffee promote teeth staining and slowly and gradually your teeth becomes yellow. Caffeine includes heavy compounds that damage the outer layer. You can switch to green tea which is light and healthier as well. Colas and sodas are acidic in nature and they are harmful to your health as well as for your teeth. These contains harmful colors and chemicals that stick to your teeth and cause damage.<br/><br/>Alcoholic drinks like vines also cause staining your teeth so if you avoid taking this you can avoid problems. If you keep your teeth white then you have to quit colas and alcoholic drinks and you can use juices in spite of this, but commercially highly treated juices also contains chemicals, so it is suggested to use only freshly squeezed juices which are not chemically treated and are good for your health and teeth as well.<br/><br/>2. Sugary Sweets:<br/><br/>Foods like sweets and chocolates also cause in discoloration. Artificial colors and chemicals used in sweets results in teeth staining. Brightly colored sweets and candies stay in your mouth for a longer time stain your teeth.<br/><br/>Chocolates are also sticky and stick to your mouth results in tooth decay and discoloration.<br/><br/>Spices and sauces are strong and again artificial colors added in it also damage your teeth. Sauces contains vinegar that is too strong and acidic also damage natural enamel. So avoid these type of food for healthier bright teeth. On the other side, you can use brightly colored fruits which may Fulfill your craving to sweet and do not damage your teeth.<br/><br/>3. Brushing:<br/><br/>There is also a misconception of brushing after eating some kind of food. You avoid this problem by brushing your teeth but this should be kept in mind not to brush direct after eating or drinking.<br/><br/>The reason of this; after drinking and eating the enamel become soft and brushing directly after this damage the outer layer so avoid brushing right after this and wait for half an hour and also use soft bristled brush to avoid this problem.<br/><br/>4. Smoking:<br/><br/>Remedies for Teeth Whitening<br/><br/>You can go to the dentist to solve this problem; otherwise there are many natural home remedies to whiten your teeth.<br/><br/>1. Baking Soda:<br/><br/>The best and powerful remedy for teeth whitening is "baking soda". Baking soda has the ability to remove stains and plaque so it will help to whiten your teeth.<br/><br/>You can use baking soda in many ways like you can mix it with your regular toothpaste or mix it with lemon or gently rub on your teeth twice a week.<br/><br/>Alternatively you can apply directly on your teeth and leave it for few seconds and rinse it with a mouthwash. This can be repeated twice in a month because excessive use of it also damage your natural enamel.<br/><br/>2. Lemon:<br/><br/>Lemons are also used as a stain remover. It has a bleaching property which removes your teeth discoloration. Lemon juice and lemon peel both are effective for teeth whitening.<br/><br/>You can mix lemon juice with your toothpaste and gently rub twice a day. You can also mix it with salt and rub on your teeth. Also you can rub lemon peel to get rid from plaque and tartar.<br/><br/>3. Salt:<br/><br/>Salt is also a quality of teeth whitening and has been used for many decades. It contains high mineral content which is helpful to retain teeth white color and also a quality of cleaning your teeth, gums and mouth as well.<br/><br/>You can use salt to clean your teeth regularly instead of toothpaste but gently rubbing is the key because rubbing it harder may damage the outer layer of your teeth.<br/><br/>4. Flossing:<br/><br/>Flossing is also important for teeth whitening and can quickly remove deposits between your teeth thus gives them a whitening look.<br/><br/>Many dentists suggest to floss your teeth twice a day for better results and they believe that flossing is more important than brushing.<br/><br/>5. Olive Oil:<br/><br/>The other tooth cleaning method is to use olive oil on your teeth. It is suggested that to apply some olive oil with a cotton swab and then after two minutes brush your teeth normally with your regular toothpaste.<br/><br/>6. Hydrogen Peroxide:<br/><br/>Hydrogen peroxide also brightens your teeth. It has also the ability to clean your teeth.<br/><br/>7. Cloves:<br/><br/>Cloves have the ability to strong your teeth as well as used for many teeth problems.<br/><br/>8. Charcoal Powder:<br/><br/>Charcoal powder is also a best teeth whitening agent. Simply put some powdered charcoal and rub your teeth and the result is awesome.<br/><br/>9. Fruit Peel:<br/><br/>Fruit peels are also a great source of teeth whitening. You can just take a banana and orange peel and gently rub the inner sides of the peels to obtain the required results.<br/><br/>Conclusion<br/><br/>So to avoid teeth discoloration you have to set a routine to stick up with these easy and fastest remedies. Your smile is worth taking and you should not to be compromise it in any situation.<br/><br/>Avoid drinking artificial drinks and foods to keep your smile brighter. You can also go to a dentist for a routine checkup to save your teeth from wearing and tearing. So keep your teeth clean and healthy and keep smiling. | Cúiseanna na mBocht Buí & 9 Leigheasanna Baile le haghaidh Méagláin<br/><br/>Is é Smile an bealach is láidre chun duine ar bith a mhealladh i dtreo tú, agus is é seo an bealach chun breathnú ort níos tarraingtí. Ach má tá tú ar an droch-dath na fiacla ná mar a bhraitheann tú náire os comhair aon duine. Cuireann fiacla bhuí droch-thionchar ar do phearsantacht agus seachnaíonn tú a aoibh gháire áit ar bith.Tá díghalráil fiacla ann go mall agus ní fhéadfadh tú é a ghlacadh dáiríre ach faoin am a d’iompaigh do fhiacla bán agus laghdaithe do mhuinín féin.<br/><br/>Ní fadhb mhór í an díolrú fiacla ach laghdaíonn sé do leibhéal muiníneach os comhair daoine.Tá go leor cúiseanna ann le mí-úsáid fiacla ach is é ceann de na príomhchúiseanna an bia a ithimid. Mura bhfuil iontógáil bia go maith; is é sin a thógaimid bia níos saorga agus nach é an bia nádúrtha ansin casfaidh sé ár bhfiacla.<br/><br/>Coimeádann na dathanna saorga i mbia ár gcuid fiacla agus ar deireadh thiar de réir an ama a thiocfaidh ár bhfiacla chun bheith buí. Bíonn ról tábhachtach ag deochanna díobhálacha óil cosúil le sóid agus tae i ndath fiacla mar go bhfuil an-ábhar de shraith cosanta damáiste sóid ar fiacla agus torthaí chun sciath cruan a lobhadh.<br/><br/>Creidmheas: Sláinte Insider<br/><br/>Níl an chúis is mó le fiacla buí ag tabhairt aire do do shláinteachas pearsanta agus ní scuabann tú é go rialta.Fiotóir aoise agus coinníollacha oidhreachtúil a bheith mar chúis is mó le mílí.<br/><br/>Is féidir leat an fhadhb seo a íoslaghdú trí na bianna sin a chuireann dí-armáil fiacla faoi deara. luaitear cuid acu thíos.<br/><br/>Cad is cúis le fiacla bhuí?<br/><br/>1. Cola, Soda agus Spóirt Deochanna:<br/><br/>Deochanna a bhfuil alcól agus caiféin acu damáiste a dhéanamh don cruan nádúrtha. Úsáid iomarcach a bhaint as tae agus caife chun na fiacla a choinneáil agus go mall de réir a chéile bíonn do chuid fiacla buí.Áiríonn Caiféin comhdhúile troma a dhéanann damáiste don ciseal seachtrach. Is féidir leat aistriú go tae glas atá éadrom agus níos sláintiúla freisin.Tá Colas agus soda aigéadach sa nádúr agus tá siad díobhálach do do shláinte chomh maith le do chuid fiacla.Tá dathanna díobhálacha agus ceimiceáin a bata chun do fiacla agus damáiste a dhéanamh.<br/><br/>Bíonn deochanna alcólacha cosúil le fíniúnacha faoi deara freisin agus do chuid fiacla á mbrú agat ionas go seachnóidh tú fadhbanna a sheachaint. Má choinníonn tú do chuid fiacla bán ansin caithfidh tú scor ó ghual agus deochanna alcólacha agus is féidir leat súnna a úsáid in ainneoin seo, ach tá ceimiceáin iontu freisin a chóireáil go h-ardaoine, agus mar sin moltar ach súnna úra brú nach gcaitear leo go ceimiceach agus atá go maith do do shláinte agus do fhiacla freisin.<br/><br/>2. milseáin mháinliachta:<br/><br/>Bíonn bianna cosúil le milseáin agus seacláidí ina gcúis le dí-armáil.Tá dathanna saorga ann agus ceimiceáin a úsáidtear i bprátaí i bpianadh fiacla.Bíonn milseáin agus candies geala daite i do bhéal ar feadh tréimhse níos faide ag fanacht le do chuid fiacla.<br/><br/>Tá seacláidí greamaitheach agus cloí le do chuid torthaí béal i lobhadh fiacail agus discoloration.<br/><br/>Tá spíosraí agus anlann láidir agus arís eile ar dathanna saorga a chuirtear leis freisin damáiste a dhéanamh do do chuid fiacla.Salainn tá fínéagar ró-láidir agus aigéadach a dhéanann damáiste do cruan nádúrtha.Mar sin, seachain an cineál bia seo le haghaidh fiacla geala sláintiúla. Ar an taobh eile, is féidir leat torthaí a bhfuil dath geal orthu a úsáid a d'fhéadfadh do craving a chomhlíonadh le milis agus nach damáiste do chuid fiacla.<br/><br/>3. Bushing:<br/><br/>Tá míthuiscint a scuabadh tar éis a ithe de chineál éigin bia.Sábhálann tú an fhadhb seo trí do chuid fiacla a scuabadh ach ba chóir é seo a choinneáil i gcuimhne gan Scuab díreach tar éis ithe nó ól.<br/><br/>An chúis atá leis seo; tar éis ól agus ag ithe an cruan a bheith bog agus scuabadh go díreach tar éis an damáiste seo a sheachaint an ciseal seachtrach a scuabadh ceart tar éis seo agus fanacht ar feadh leath uair an chloig agus freisin scuab brettled bog a úsáid chun an fhadhb seo a sheachaint.<br/><br/>4. Caitheamh tobac:<br/><br/>Leigheasanna do Fiacla whitening<br/><br/>Féadfaidh tú dul chuig an bhfiaclóir chun an fhadhb seo a réiteach; mura bhfuil go leor leigheasanna baile nádúrtha ann chun do chuid fiacla a ghealú.<br/><br/>1. Briseadh Soda:<br/><br/>Is é an leigheas is fearr agus cumhachtach do fiacla whitening "saking soda".Tá an cumas a stains agus plaic a bhaint mar sin beidh sé cabhrú le whiten do fiacla a ghlanadh.<br/><br/>Is féidir leat sóid bácála a úsáid ar go leor bealaí is féidir leat é a mheascadh le do taos fiacla rialta nó é a mheascadh le líomóid nó go réidh rub ar do chuid fiacla dhá uair sa tseachtain.<br/><br/>Nó is féidir leat iarratas a dhéanamh go díreach ar do chuid fiacla agus é a fhágáil ar feadh cúpla soicind agus é a sruthlaithe le béal.Is féidir é seo a athdhéanamh dhá uair sa mhí toisc go ndéanann sé damáiste do cruan nádúrtha freisin.<br/><br/>2. Lemon:<br/><br/>Tá maoin tuaradh a bhaineann do fiacla discoloration.Tá sú líomóide agus craiceann líomóide éifeachtach do whitening fiacla freisin.Tá sé ina chúis le cóireáil den chineál is cúis le díslí nádúrtha agus freisin le dath an tae.<br/><br/>Is féidir leat sú líomóide a mheascadh le do taos fiacla agus go réidh rub dhá uair sa lá.Is féidir leat é a mheascadh le salann agus rub ar do chuid fiacla freisin.Is féidir leat craiceann líomóide a rub chun fáil réidh le plaic agus tartar.<br/><br/>3. Salann:<br/><br/>Tá salann freisin ar chaighdeán na fiacla agus tá sé in úsáid le blianta fada anuas.Tá ábhar mianraí ard ann a chuidíonn le dath bán fiacla a choinneáil agus cáilíocht do chuid fiacla, gumaí agus béil a ghlanadh freisin.<br/><br/>Is féidir leat salann a úsáid chun do chuid fiacla a ghlanadh go rialta in ionad taos fiacla ach is é an eochair é a chuimilt toisc go bhféadfadh sé damáiste níos deacra a dhéanamh do chiseal seachtrach do chuid fiacla.<br/><br/>4. Fosing:<br/><br/>Tá Flossing freisin tábhachtach do fiacla a whitening agus is féidir a bhaint go tapa taiscí idir do fiacla sin tugann siad breathnú whitening.<br/><br/>Molann go leor fiaclóirí do chuid fiacla a floss dhá uair sa lá le haghaidh torthaí níos fearr agus creideann siad go bhfuil flossing níos tábhachtaí ná scuabadh.<br/><br/>5. Ola olóige:<br/><br/>Is é an modh eile glantacháin fiacail ola olóige a úsáid ar do chuid fiacla.Moltar go gcuirfí roinnt ola olóige i bhfeidhm le swab cadáis agus ansin tar éis dhá nóiméad scuab do chuid fiacla le do théatáit rialta.<br/><br/>6. sárocsaíd hidrigine:<br/><br/>Déanann sárocsaíd hidrigine do chuid fiacla a ghealú freisin.Tá an cumas aige do chuid fiacla a ghlanadh.<br/><br/>7. Cloíonn:<br/><br/>Tá sé de chumas ag lámhainní do chuid fiacla a neartú chomh maith le go leor fadhbanna fiacla a úsáid.<br/><br/>8. Púdar gualaigh:<br/><br/>Is gníomhaire whitening is fearr é púdar gualaigh freisin.Cuir roinnt gualaigh púdraithe agus rub do chuid fiacla agus tá an toradh uamhnach.<br/><br/>9. Torthaí Peel:<br/><br/>Is foinse iontach fiacla iad na peels torthaí freisin. Ní féidir leat ach craiceann banana a thógáil agus a eagrú agus taobh istigh na craiceann a chuimil go réidh chun na torthaí riachtanacha a fháil.<br/><br/>Conclúid<br/><br/>Mar sin chun mílí fiacla a sheachaint caithfidh tú gnáthamh a shocrú chun na leigheasanna seo atá éasca agus is gasta.Is fiú do aoibh gháire a thógáil agus níor cheart duit a bheith comhréiteach in aon chás.<br/><br/>Seachain deochanna agus bianna saorga a ól chun do chuid bia a choinneáil níos gile.Is féidir leat dul chuig fiaclóir le haghaidh gnáth seiceála chun do chuid fiacla a shábháil ó chaitheamh agus tearing.Mar sin coinnigh do chuid fiacla glan agus sláintiúil agus coinnigh miongháire. |
| Jeans, the iconic garment of your wardrobe!<br/><br/>A "closet must" - Jeans can be seen on catwalks or worn by just about anyone on the street.<br/><br/>It dresses all silhouettes and finds its place in women's, men's and kid's wardrobes. Available in several colours and cuts, jeans remain the best-selling garment, with 73 pairs sold every second in the world.<br/><br/>Jeans became popular in the 1850s, with Levis' famous 501 model. But the creation of this garment dates back to the 16th century.<br/><br/>Falsely, "jeans" are often referred to as a fashion item. This multipurpose word is used to describe the famous pair of blue pants, but this use really outshines its essential meaning: its fabric. Indeed, what we commonly call "jeans" happens to be a fabric (denim), which differs from the actual jeans "garment". | Jeans, an ball éadaigh íocónach de do wardrobe!<br/><br/>A "daltais" - Is féidir le Jeans le feiceáil ar catwalks nó caite ag díreach faoi dhuine ar bith ar an tsráid.<br/><br/>Gúnaí sé gach scáthchruth agus fhaigheann a áit i mban ar, fir agus leanaí wardrobes.Ar fáil i roinnt dathanna agus ciorruithe, tá jeans an éadaigh is fearr-díol, le 73 péirí dhíol gach dara ar fud an domhain.<br/><br/>Tháinig an-tóir ar Jeans sna 1850idí, agus samhail cáiliúil 501 Levis. Ach téann cruthú an éadaigh seo siar go dtí an 16ú haois.<br/><br/>Ar ndóigh, "jeans" go minic dá ngairtear mír faisin.Úsáidtear an focal ilchuspóireach seo chun cur síos a dhéanamh ar an bpéir cáiliúil de pants gorm, ach leagann an úsáid seo amach a bhrí riachtanach i ndáiríre: a fhabraic. Go deimhin, a bhfuil ar a dtugtar go coitianta "jeans" a tharlaíonn a bheith ina fabraic (denim), atá difriúil ó na jeans iarbhír " éadaigh". |
|  for real results of reconciliation have slowly chipped away at these stereotypes but these remarks still leave a lasting mark on the Native community in Canada.<br/><br/>Introduction<br/><br/>Orlando, The Marmalade Cat, A Seaside Holiday by Kathleen Hale is a very appealing children's book originally introduced in the 1900s. To give a quick overview of the book, it is about an orange cat, Orlando (Marmalade since he is orange) who goes on a family trip<br/><br/>Orlando, The Marmalade Cat, A Seaside Holiday by Kathleen Hale cover. Published by Country Life & Puffin Picture Books between 1938-1972.<br/><br/>to a beach. During their trip things get very interesting and adventurous as they begin to swim underwater and find a lost shipwreck as well as a queen who had been there for a long time. The book has several colorful images alongside the text giving younger readers more engagement when reading the book. These images are present in different sizes, some being small to half a page large, where at one point we have an image<br/><br/>covering a full 2 pages. The goal of this digital exhibit is to further analyze the examine the use of images in this book and how they appeal to a child's development and understanding through reading. It will be looked through both the images and detail used, as well as how and where these images are used within the text. Pictures not only play a role in engaging an audience into the story, but it also serves as a funnel of extra meaning and clarification beside text.<br/><br/>The role of images<br/><br/>An image itself is a very important aspect to a book. It may bring life to a book, it sets a setting in a reader's head of what the story "looks" like. Especially when it comes to a child who's imagination can run wild and any moment, it has a significant impact on how they view the story and what they are able to extract from it. Images do not solely act as an extension for entertainment and imaginary thoughts for children, there is an educational factor to it as well. Children are able to view an image, relate it to the text that is related to it, and then extract information from that. For example if there is a picture book about animals and the text speaks about camouflage, there is then an image of a chameleon camouflaging on a tree. When a child views this image, they get that final understand of that camouflage is and what it looks like. From that image and text, they then are able to extract that knowledge into the real world. A study conducted by Patricia A. Ganea, Judy S. DeLoache, and Lili Ma consisted of showing children images of animals with camouflage in picture books. Afterwards they are then shown pictures of animals and asked which animals were most likely to fall prey in which case the animals that did not have camouflage traits were chosen (Ganea, DeLoache, and Ma, 1). This study importantly concludes that images in a children's picture book have much more purpose than a simple "fun" factor. Children are able to learn through their reading experience and transfer that knowledge into the real world.<br/><br/>How spacing is used<br/><br/>Space is something that usually lies subconsciously within one's mind while reading a book with pictures. When you read a picture book you are not actively trying to figure out how the images take up a certain space and what that means. Well let me extract the importance of space in text. The use of space does not technically have a direct meaning to it, but rather it is to be examined through the whole text. Space can give clues about a story, it can foreshadow events, it can highlight important moments in a story, and it can be progressive. In the article "The Journey Through the 'Space in the Text' to Where the Wild Things Are" by Ann Moseley it is described that the way images use space in a text may<br/><br/>A 2 page image from Maurice Sendak's Where the Wild Things Are, [New York]: Harper & Row,1963, SlideShare LinkedIn Corporation, 27 Feb. 2012,  off clues and provide further analysis of a story. For example in Where the Wild Things Are, the images of the story begin small and grow in size as the plot progresses until we have a full 2 page image. Afterwards, the images then begin to shrink in size during the denouement of the story until the final image is shown which is larger in size than the first. When analyzed, the images are in fact tied directly to the protagonist's development. He starts off with a small image, meaning a clean slate. When the story finishes, he ends up with a bit of knowledge gained through his experience which is shown by the slightly larger final image (Moseley, 86-87). Although this progression cannot be understood at first, when the images are analyzed further taking the text into context, we can see how important that images use up space in specific ways.<br/><br/>Orlando's adaptations to images and space<br/><br/>In Orlando, The Marmalade Cat, A Seaside Holiday, the images that are used feature animals using very soft colors which are appealing to the eyes. There are not any super sharp edges or lines, overall the images used are very soft which gives a very smooth sort of feel to it for a reader. What's important about the use of the colors and image style here is how a child would feel when reading the book. An article titled "Children Reading Pictures: Interpreting Visual Texts, Taylor and Francis, 2002." by Arizpe, Evelyn, and Morag<br/><br/>An almost full page of an image taken from Orlando, The Marmalade Cat, A Seaside Adventure, featuring a ship in the form of a cat, taken from Babyccinokids.com.<br/><br/>gives some insight in how children extract information from images. They conducted a study using children of different ages and backgrounds where they were assessed on their ability to draw meaning from images. Results showed that they were able to extract not only meaning while relating it to the text, but also get a sense of the mood and realism involved (Arizpe, Evelyn, & Morag, 2002). The use of these smooth images and colors in Orlando will definitely allowed children viewers to grasp mood from it and therefore getting more sensation from an image as opposed to simply understanding it's contents. Moreover; children tend to enjoy picture books that feature dominant animal characters as it may be more imaginative and adventurous as opposed to books about only human characters (Ganea, Patricia A., et al, 1425-1428). Although Orlando does not follow a specific progression of images such that Where the Wild Things Are does, space definitely is considered when images are placed. The images used perfectly relate to the text supporting it which make it very easy for a reader to understand, however some parts of the story are given more importance for instance where we have almost 2 full pages of images sometimes. These images stand out and have more meaning and importance than the rest due to its largeness.<br/><br/>Significance<br/><br/>In conclusion, I believe we can all agree that images play a very important role in a children's book. These images being colorful and detailed in nature bring out the imagination of a child. Moreover; children are able to extract further information and detail from images where they can bring it with them into the real world. Besides the image itself, how the image is placed can be analyzed for clues and hidden information about a story. It may not be obvious at first, but as further analysis is done we can conclude that images play a key role in the development of a story.<br/><br/>Images in this online exhibit are either in the public domain or being used under fair dealing for the purpose of research and are provided solely for the purposes of research, private study, or education.<br/><br/>Since When Did Dreaming of Becoming a Princess be so Scary?<br/><br/>When I was a kid, I dreamt of becoming a princess like the ones I read from fairy tale books. I imagined getting rescued from a locked tower by a knight in shining armor who goes by the name Prince Charming. The prince would ride on a horse with his wavy and suave hair, wearing perfectly aligned, white teeth. In my head, it was very magical and romantic.<br/><br/>Therefore, it did not even occur in my mind that something so small like a pocket book of Sandy Posner's The Sleeping Princess (The Story of the Ballet) would present to be a bombshell due to its rather problematic content as a feminist text…!<br/><br/>This is the second edition of the picture book published in 1949 by Adam and Charles Black; its first publication date being 1945 established by Newman Wolsey Ltd.<br/><br/>It consists of images illustrated by Joyce Millen. This book was considered to be popular because of the rapid interest in ballet dance throughout the European countries during its publication period (Posner 7). It is based off of "La Belle au bois Dormant" (Posner 20), the French version of Sleeping Beauty: a known classical tale that portrays an enchanting love-story about a prince who wakes up a sleeping princess with a kiss.<br/><br/>Seemingly harmless at this point; a kiss is no threat. However, beyond this book's manifestation is a latent encouragement for sexual exploitation imposed on young dreamers of females.<br/><br/>In The Sleeping Princess, we will look at how the prince comes to kiss the princess, what role the princess initially has, and how the readers are supposed to perceive their characterizations.<br/><br/>"Of all fairy tales Sleeping Beauty is perhaps the most cinematic in its fashioning of a primal scene for visual pleasure" (Maria Tartar 143)<br/><br/>Formatting the Story Book<br/><br/>Posner tells the story of The Sleeping Princess in the format of a descriptive ballet play. Staying true to its form as a ballet book, Posner incorporates ballet terms like "arabesque" (80), a ballet posture, and "mazurka" (96), a group ballet dance. Instead of saying "they lived happily ever after" which is often how fairy-tales end their story, Posner ends the story with "the curtain falls" (96).<br/><br/>These traits depict The Sleeping Princess as a creative and sensual revision of the classical tale that should appeal to readers who are fans of ballet based on the book's particularly unique references. It is using a "cinematic" design from how the story is told in motion of ballet dances, while the illustrations act as support with their "visual" effects.<br/><br/>"Curiosity and the desire to look mingle with a display that is both aesthetically and erotically charged" (Tartar 143)<br/><br/>The Female Gender Role<br/><br/>Note how Princess Aurora is illustrated elegantly with a very slim figure, focusing on her long bare legs (seen in Figure 2). Her bed chamber is also emphasized with royal drapes of crowns but at the same time induces a very inviting look (Figure 1 & 3). Princess Aurora is presented as a sexual object.<br/><br/>In appearance, this book may seem modest but it's actually an "erotic" depiction of the female lead's character that subjects her to a case of vulnerability. Based on Leslee Farish Kuykendal and Brian W. Sturm's outline on role reversal, there is reference to Princess Elizabeth by Robert Munsch from The Paperbag Princess released on 1980, as an example of a female character that crosses literary borders in comparison to Aurora's conventional character. Princess Elizabeth is the one doing the rescuing in the story by marching to the tower to face the presumed antagonist, a dragon, demanding for the release of Prince Ronald. Thus, she is portraying a strong and valiant female character in "reversal" to how children usually read the depiction of womanly roles (Kuykendal & Sturm 40).<br/><br/>In contrast, Aurora represents the conventional female character due to her docile behaviour. She lacks the agency to choose her own destiny by sleeping throughout the tale. Unaware of the things happening in time, she only has one duty which is to wait for the right prince who would save her from the sleeping curse and marry that said man. Looking at the publication year of both texts, it is important to note that The Sleeping Princess was released before The Paper Bag Princess.
